<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <div style="max-width:100%;margin-left:0%; margin-right:0%;border:solid 1px;background-color:;;padding-top:2pt;padding-bottom:3pt">
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; padding-top:0pt; margin-left:1%; margin-right:1%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>The following communications will be posted to ExxonMobil corporate and affiliate social media accounts
and may be used in other communications materials. </I></P></div> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" ALIGN="center">

<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">
<TD VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="center"><B>ENERGY FACTOR</B></TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>VISUAL </U></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">


<IMG SRC="g178892g0422095453839.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Earth Day 2021: Our People and Their Stories </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Earth Day presents an opportunity to reflect upon the work of providing energy that is essential to improving lives around the world while managing the risks
of climate change. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ExxonMobil researchers, scientists and operators around the world share that same vision. Some of their work involves researching new
materials to capture carbon dioxide, finding innovative ways to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">re-use</FONT> recyclable plastic material, <U>improving energy efficiency and reducing emissions from the company&#146;s operations</U>.<U> </U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Here&#146;s a look at some of those people and their stories. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Video: </B><U>https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=feCXFEixlI4</U> </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">


<IMG SRC="g178892g0422095454088.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Transcript: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Across the
world, ExxonMobil employees work tirelessly to reduce emissions and work towards a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-carbon</FONT> future. Here are some of those stories and that work&#133; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">My name is Matt Kapelewski and I&#146;m a materials researcher in Clinton, NJ. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">My name is Inge Daems and I work at the European Technology Center in Brussels. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">My name is Angela Ang<B> </B>and I work in Singapore. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">My name is
Carla Periera and I am based in Clinton, NJ. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">My name is Cody Hays and I work in the Permian Basin. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">My name is Shwetha&nbsp;Ramkumar and I work in Houston, Texas. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">I
am committed to a lower-carbon future by helping to scale new carbon capture technologies. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#133;by making manufacturing less energy-intensive </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#133;through lowering emissions from natural gas production </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#133;through energy optimization </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#133;with reduced plastic waste </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">I am committed to a lower-carbon future, with new technologies in drilling and hydrocarbon productions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In my role, I find new ways to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">re-use</FONT> recycled plastic material by working with manufacturers that use ExxonMobil
polymers </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">I test and design breakthrough materials that could provide a lower-emissions future by fundamentally changing how we capture carbon dioxide.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">I research how new technologies today can help refineries and chemical plants cut their energy use as well as our carbon dioxide footprint. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">It&#146;s work that involves finding new technologies &#150; like aerial surveillance and ground-based sensors. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">I identify opportunities to drive energy efficiently in our refining operations. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">I apply new technology that can help our upstream operations reduce their carbon dioxide footprint </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">at the heart of my work is a pledge to my children that I am working to impact their future. That is energizing and motivating. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We may face setbacks along the way, but we are committed to cracking this science. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">It&#146;s about spreading the mindset of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-ownership</FONT> and continuous improvement to challenge existing norms and
uncover new ideas. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Delivering the energy we need in our everyday lives is essential to the growth we see around us, but doing so with fewer emissions is
very important for a lower-carbon world. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We are committed to our mission to harness advanced technologies that can monitor and track methane so we can
curb those emissions </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">That is what makes us work harder </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">I&#146;m proud to be part of that work </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Every day is Earth
Day&#151;let&#146;s share our stories. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g178892g0422095454385.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P>
</DIV></Center>

holdings or otherwise is set forth in the Proxy Statement. To the extent holdings of such participants in ExxonMobil&#146;s securities are not reported, or have changed since the amounts described, in the Proxy Statement, such changes have been
reflected on Initial Statements of Beneficial Ownership on Form 3 or Statements of Change in Ownership on Form 4 filed with the SEC. Details concerning the nominees of ExxonMobil&#146;s Board of Directors for election at the 2021 Annual Meeting are

ANY SUPPLEMENTS THERETO AND ACCOMPANYING BLUE PROXY CARD, BECAUSE THEY CONTAIN IMPORTANT INFORMATION. Investors and shareholders can obtain a copy of the Proxy Statement and other relevant documents filed by ExxonMobil free of charge from the
